151b6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyang bar bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam rnam par dag pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/
151b7(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ skyon med par sems can gyi khams yongs su smin par bya ba'i smon lam dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba sna tshogs bsags pas 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su dag par bya ba'i
151b8(phal chen): smon lam dang / lus dang srog gis bsngo ning dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pa'i lham dang / ye shes kyi sgo rnam par sbyang ba khong du chud pas/ sangs rgyas kyi ning la 'jug pa'i sro
152a1(phal chen): lam dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang gnyis su med pas tshul gcig gi rgyud du 'gro ba'i smon lam dang / de bzhir gshegs pa'i sgol 'jug
152a2(phal chen): pas chos thams cad khong du chud pa'i smon lam dang / mos pa rnams par sbyangs ngas bstan don yod pa'i smon lam dang / phyi ma'i mtha' byin gyis brlabs pas bskal par gnas pa'i
152a3(phal chen): smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang ngo'i theg pa'i rgyan rnam pa thams cad kyi sgonas rnam par snang ba'i sngon lam dag ste/ kye hral ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa'
152a4(phal chen): rnams ni de ltar smon lam rnam par spyong ngo // de dag rnam pa bcus smon lam yongs su rdzogs par byed de/ bcu gang nen/ yongs su slob med pa dang / rkun chen po mngon par
152a5(phal chen): bsgrub pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam khyad par du 'phags pa rnams kyi rjes su 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i
152a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing thos nas/ rang gi smor lam du mngon par sgrub pa dang / bsam pa phyi ma'i tha'i mur thug pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba btugs
152a7(phal chen): ma'i smon lam chen po dang ldan pa dang / bcas pa thams cad du gnas pas mi 'jigs pa dang / sdug bsngal thams cad kyis ji misnyapa pa dang / bde bams cad lo ye mi
152a8(phal chen): pa dang / bsam pa mnyam pa med pa'i rnam par thar pa yongs su srung dag rtse/ de dag smon la mchen zi ltar yongs su spong cing yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas mcho
152b1(phal chen): ba'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// gzugs 'khrul pa med pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// smon lam zang mi zhes pas chos thams cad zin tu rtogs pa'i
152b2(phal chen): gzungs kyang rab tu thob bo// snying rje chen pos 'gro ba thams cad yongs su skyob pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyud kyi gter zad mi shes pa 'dra rab
152b3(phal chen): tu 'thob bo// 'gro ba thams cad tshim par bya ba'i bsod nams kyi gter zeng ma shes pa'ang rab tu shes 'thob bo// chos thams cad yang dag pa ji lta bu bzhin du brtag pa'i ye shes
152b4(phal chen): kyi gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu thob bo// rnam par smin pa la gnas pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob po// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs mtha'
152b5(phal chen): yas pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' dang dbus med par gtogs pa la 'jug pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu thob bo// de ltar
152b6(phal chen): gter rab tu thob cing bsod nams dang ye shes kyi cho gas zad mi shes pa dang ldan pa de dag ye shes chen po'i dkyil 'khor yongs su dag pas/ sems can rnams la bsam pa ji lta ba
152b7(phal chen): bzhin du chos kyi gter gyi sbyin pa byed do// kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du ji ltar 'jug ce na/ sbyor bstong ba dang
152b8(phal chen): mi bral ba dang / rim gyis bsam gtan dang ting nge 'dzin mngon par bsgrub pa dang / gnas med cing blang ba med pa shin tu rtog pa dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad rab tu sel ba dang /
153a1(phal chen): ting nge badzin gyi sgo tha' las mngon par bsgrub pa dang / mngon pa shes pa cher pos rnam da baphrul pa'i rjes su 'gro ba dang / rim gyis rnam par spong pa
153a2(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin gyi sgol rab tu 'jug pa dang / ting nge 'dzin cig la sgo mtha' yas par rab tu 'jug pa dang / ting 'dzin gyi spyod yul thams cad shes pa dang / de'i yul gyi rjes su rab tu
153a3(phal chen): zhugs pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa thams cad ye shes kyi phyag rgya mi khrugs pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i sa la nye bar gyur pas/ bsam gtan gyi gyi pha rol tu phyin pas
153a4(phal chen): yongs su dag par byed do// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mnyam pa dang / gzung ba dang / blang ba dang / bcang ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad bsnyen bkur bas yongs

153a6(phal chen): bral ba dang / chos thams cad rnam par 'byed pa la mkhas pa dang / mtshan nyid kyi phyag rna mi dad pa dang / de bzhin bzhigs pa'i sgonas lhun gyis grub par gro ning rnam
153a7(phal chen): bsgom pa dang / stobs la 'jug pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la 'jug pacun mi 'chad pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo kun dang ldan pas thams cad mkhyen
153a8(phal chen): 'i sor 'jug brgyan mi che nga dang / shes rabakyi 'ol phyin pa sgo kun dang ldan pas thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgor 'jug pas/ shes rab kyi ril tu phyin pa yongs su dag par
153b1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi bya ba'i rgyud thams cad stod pa dang / sems cad gyi rlung yongs su smin pas yongasu mi skyo ba dang / bsam pa bzhin du bye bstod pa dang / bya ba thams cad la mngon par
153b2(phal chen): chags pa med pa dang / byis pa'i stong pa dang / 'phags pa'i spyod pa bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa dang / 'khor bar du mya ngan las 'das panye bar ston pa dang / sbyor ba
153b3(phal chen): thams cad shin tu brtags pas rgyu bdang rgan thams cad bstan pa gnas med pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi rjes su 'gro ning rjes su 'brang ba dang / sems can thams cad sgrom
153b4(phal chen): ba'i spod pas thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su spong ngo // sems can gyi khams mthar thug pa yongs su smin par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams mthar thug pa yongs
153b5(phal chen): su sbyang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thar thug par mchod pa dang / tshe chags pa med pa'i mthar thug par rnam par 'chang rgya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyis mthar thug par spyod pa'i
153b6(phal chen): dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / bskal pa phyi ma'i mthar thug par rab tu gnas pa dang / sems bskyed pa'i mthar thug par stobs la 'jug pa dang / 'gro ba
153b7(phal chen): dang ldog pa mthar thug par mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / zhing gi gnas kyi mthar thug par thams cad mthong ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi mthar thug par rab tu tho
153b8(phal chen): par bye bas smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do// bsam pa'i stobs kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa'i stobs dbang du gyur cing thob
154a1(phal chen): pa med pa dang snying rje chen po'i stobs skyo ba med pa dang / byams pa chen po'i stobs snyoms pa'i sbyor ba can dang / gzungs kyi stobs dor thams cad kyi
154a2(phal chen): sbyor ba la bsgribs pa med pa dang / spobs pa'i stobs 'gro ba thams cad tshim par byed pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i stobs theg pa thams cad kyi rgyan byed pa dang / smod lam
154a3(phal chen): gyi stobs bcad du mi rung ba dang / mngon par shes pa'i stobs chad med pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi byid kyi brlabs la mos pa dam pa'i stobs rab tu 'dzin pas
154a4(phal chen): stobs pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do// 'dod chags kyi spyod pa khongs du chud pa dang / ne sdang gi spyod pa rjes su rtogs pa dang / gti mug gi spyod parab tu rtog pa dang /
154a5(phal chen): chamanyam pa'i spyod pa rjes su shes pa dang / slob pa'i sems kyi spyod pa rab du rtogs pa dang / skad cig gcig gis sems can mtha' yas pa'i spyod pa rnams par zlog pa dang / sems
154a6(phal chen): dang bsam pa mtha' yas pa thams cad shes par byed pa dang / chos thams cad la yang dag pa jis pa bzhin du rtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rjes 'jug pa dang

154a8(phal chen): de ga sa sa rgyad ba ngas ngas sa kyang zhing sa phyin pa dag yongs su rnags par byed pa dang / ro dun phyogs pa lajing byang chung sems pa'i seg pa che po'i sa
154b1(phal chen): ldan pa la gnas shing sems can gyi khams ji ltar dam bcas pa bzhin du yang dag par sgrol lo// de dag dge ba'i las shin tu bsags pa ston pas ngan song du 'gro ba'i sems can sgrol
154b2(phal chen): brtsam pa chen po la gzung bas sems can gyi khams mi khom par 'gro ba stsol lo// lhag mthong nye bar stabs pas gzugs kyi khams na khong pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol lo//
154b3(phal chen): phra ba'i ye shes nye bar bsabs pas gzugs med pa'i khams su skyes pa'i sems can rnams bskol lo// ni ba'i tshul nye bar bsangs pas nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa
154b4(phal chen): la mos pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol lo// stobs bcu'i rgyan chen po dang ldan pa bstan pas theg pa chen po la mos pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol lo// de ltar na sngon las dang po'i
154b5(phal chen): sal gnas pa'i tshe/ sems can g.yang sa chen po nas lhung ba rnam pa tha dad par gyur pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes te/ sgo sna tshogs nas zung bar bya'o// nes seng ge'i sgras sbags pa de
154b6(phal chen): bzhin du ye shes thob pa rnams sems can thams cad bskal ba'i rab tu zhugs pa yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' ye shes ji lta bu la zhugs pa ni rtag tu rgyun mi gcod
154b7(phal chen): par sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / chos kyi rigs dang / dge 'dun gyi'i gas mi chad pa'i phyir zhugs pa yin te/ de dag byang chub sems gnan gyi sems kyi rgyud la gnog pas sangs
154b8(phal chen): rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ chos kyi mdzod rnam par 'grel pas chos kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ bstan pa'i tshul dang 'gal bar mi byed pas/ dge 'dun gyi rigs mi
155a1(phal chen): gcod pa yid/ smon lam chen po yang dag par brjod pas/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i tshul yang dag par ston pa/

191b1(phal chen): tsani re re la yang kha'i sgo bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa brjod du med pa yod par gyur te/ sems can gcig ji lta bar sems can de dag thams cad kyang de baning du
191b2(phal chen): de snyed kyi kha'i sgo dang ldan la/ sems can de dag thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa' la skad du brjod pa// khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa rnam par rtags pas/ dus
191b3(phal chen): gcig tu byas te/ yongs su dri bar byas kyang byang chub sems dpa' ni de lta bu'i sems can gcig ras gcig tu rgyud pa dang / de lta bu'i skad cig ras gcig tu brgyud pa dang / de
191b4(phal chen): bu'i brjod pa sna tshogs kyis yongs su dris pa la'ang chos gzung ba la thogs pa med pa yin/ brjod pa shes pa'i phyir rnam par rtog pa med pa yin te/ dris pa'i the tshom yongs su ngas

191b6(phal chen): 'di snyam du sems so// gal te skra'i rtse mo re re la sems bskyed pa re re ning 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor brjod du med pa zhig byung la/ sems skad cig re re la rtog pa gzhan dang gzhan gyis

192a1(phal chen): par 'byung la/ skye ba'i rgyud mi chud pa zhig yod du zin ra yang bstan par bya ba'i sa de la byang chub sems dpa' sems skad cig 'ga' tsam du yang num pa mi skye'o//

192a3(phal chen): dpa'i chos bzang po la gnas pa de ni 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis sems can 'di dag dang / sems can gnan rnams dang sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi tshig gi la
192a4(phal chen): gyis yongs su 'gu bar byas te/ chos bzhud pa'i mthar thug par mi bya// chos la rnam par thogs par mi bya'o// nas nas ngas brjod pa de dag thams cad kyang rab tu shes te/ sem

192b4(phal chen): ba med pa'i lus rnams dang / 'gro ba thams cad du 'byung bas mtha' yas par 'gro ba'i lus rnams dang mi skye ba dang mnyam pa'i chos la brtson pas ma skyes pa'i lus rnams

193a6(phal chen): dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dgu pa'i nas bzang po nas bya ba ste/ de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi chos

193b1(phal chen): par byed de smra'o// de 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sde bden pa'i gsung la srung / ma byor pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bded pa'i gsang 'ang ma na

193b6(phal chen): su slob pa'i ye shes dang ldan pas gnyis su med par smras pa yin no// de sems can rnams kyi gnas ma yin pa'i ye shes pa la'ang rab tu 'jug go// de sems can rnams kyi 'angs pa
193b7(phal chen): dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i las rnam par smin pa shes pa la'ang rab tu 'jug go/ dbang po dang brtson 'grus rnam par dad pa/ rdzogs pa dang ma rdzogs pa dang / rab dang tha ma shes

194a1(phal chen): ba'i lam gyi ye shes la'ang rab tu 'jug go// bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / stobs par 'jug pa dang / kun nas non mongs pa

194a7(phal chen): med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi mthas btugs par 'gyur ba dang / gang 'di phung po'i lhag ma lus pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings kyi mthar thug par gnas

194b1(phal chen): yang dag par zhugs pa/ sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba la thog mar 'gro ba'o// bdag cag ni thams cad mkhyen pa zhid la 'jug pa'i phyir 'khor lo bsgyur ba ste/ bdag

197b1(phal chen): jo bo nyid kyis zhugs gyur pa'i// bde gshegs gzhan dring mi 'jog pa// mkha' mnyam de dag spyong pa 'di yin no// 'jig rten kun tu mtha' yas pa// mamakha' klas pa yang dag thun
197b2(phal chen): sra chud 'gyur te// zil gyis gnon chos mnga' ba thub mchog de dag spyod pa 'di yin no// ldog pa med pa de dag rnams// mi mnga' chos dang ldan pa thug par dka' ba dang // smo mapa snangs
197b3(phal chen): kyi mthar phyin pa// spyod legs mnga' ba'i spyod 'di mnyan par gyis// mtha' dang dbus no med pa sar// rjes su zhugs shing thams cad gzigs par gyur pa rnams// spyod yul bzung na
197b4(phal chen): mngara' ba yi// smra ba'i seng ge'i spyod pa 'di yin no// rab tu dbye ba'i tshig rgyus la// rjes su zhugs zhing rgyal ba 'dul bar mdzad pa yi// chos rnams rtogs pa mnga' ba rnams// thub chen/
197b5(phal chen): de dag spyod pa 'di yin no// thams cad bde ba bskyed mdzad cing // sems can nyes med thugs dang ldan pa rnams// kha lo bsgyur ba mnyam pa'i yon tan tshad med de dag spyod 'di yin/
197b6(phal chen): 'jigs pa med pa stobs mdzad cing // sems can thams cad rab tu tshim pa rnams// rang zhing rnyog pa med pa yi// dpa' med de dag spyod pa 'di yin no// dge ba'i thugs dang ldan pa
197b7(phal chen): rnams bsam pa rnam par dag cing spros pa'i dpal gyi gzi brjid spungs rgyas pa// dpal mchog ldan pa de dag sbyong 'di'o// don gyi pha rol phyin pa'i rnams// yon tan 'byung gam
197b8(phal chen): rnam par dag pa'i thugs mnga' ba// shin tu sems pa'i blo ldan rnams// srid nas 'phags pa de dag spyod 'di'o// bdag med nyams pa med pa rnams// rnga'i dbyangs rab mnga'
198a1(phal chen): ning du gnol pa dang // chos kyi tshul la gnas pa rnams// tshig la nyams med de dag spyod 'di'o// sbyir bas shin tu 'phags pa'i rnams// bsod nams ma/
198a2(phal chen): rab brgyas kyang rab tu brgyan pa dag/ 'grol phan par mdzad pa rnams// blo rab de dag spyod yul 'di yin no// ye shes shin tu zab pa'i sar// rjes su zhugs shing blo gros shin tu ga
198a3(phal chen): pa rnams// mi g.yol brtan zhing gnas pa dag/ brtul zhugs brtan pa de dag spyod 'di'o// chos kyi dbyings la' mjug pa yin// rjes su 'jug pha rol phyin par gyur pa dag
198a4(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul la brtson pa rnams// chos kyi nyi ma de dge sbyong 'di'o// mi mnyam mnyam pa'i blo mnga' rnams// mi mnyam yongs su bsgoms pa'i ting 'dzin ldan// bsam pa/
198a5(phal chen): na tu rtogs pa dag/ thams cad gzigs pa de dag sbyod 'do'o// 'jig rtem khas la rab 'jug pa// bru dang yangs dang d+ha che'i rnam pa thams cad du// snod sul thob par gyur
198a6(phal chen): rnams ye shes ra bong dag spyong 'dig/ yongs su rig pa'i sems ldan pa// khams rnams gsum po kungan tu chags pa med pa dag/ tshul khrims bcu'i thugs mthar phyir pa/
198a7(phal chen): rnam dge sems ldan de dag slong 'dig// rnamakha' byangs kyi mangs btugs pa// ye shes 'byam klas mngon sum brjod du med pal// zhugs te srabs pa'i blo ldan pa/

198b2(phal chen): dpal chen de dag spyod 'dri'o// sems can mtha' dang dbus med pa// phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten dag na rgyu bar gyur pa rnams// sems can kun gyi bdag ni skyabs yin pa// 'jigs
198b3(phal chen): med de dag spyong pa 'di yin no// rtag par brtson 'grus nas 'tshal zhing // nam yang sangs rgyas chos la num pa med pa rnams// de ni 'jig nen spyad phyir te// klu chen de dag spyong pa

198b5(phal chen): 'di'o// phyogs rnams bcu por tshad med pa'i// mtha' dang dbus med rin chen mang pos 'grengs byed kyang // nam yang spyod pa'i yid med pa// dang par byed pa de dag spyod 'a

199a2(phal chen): med pa// byang chub rab la gzhol zhing spyad pa spyod pa dang // yon tan thams cad mthar phyin pa// legs pa mi zad de dag spyod 'di'o// 'jig rten 'das pa'i smra ba rnams smra ba'i dam pa smras

199b7(phal chen): bsags pa rnams// ye shes skyob pa bsod nams chen po'i snying po can// bsod nams mu stegs 'gro ba yi// sems can dam pa'i spyod 'di'o// chos dbyings kun

230a5(phal chen): tu bkye/ gzugs parnam pa sna tshogs kyi char ni rab tu ba ba/ lha rdzas kyis gos rab ma pa'i srin ni rab tu brtse/ rin pa che yid du 'ong ba mtha' yas pa thams cad kyi sprin gyi ni
230a6(phal chen): rab tu ba ba/ sems shin tu dang bas su rdzas kyi sku bsgru ba dang / mtsho 'phrul gyi sprin gyi char ni rab tub ba/ bcug spos rnam pa du ma'i sprin gyis ni kun tu gdugs/ sgra rdzas kyi
230a7(phal chen): tsan dan gyi bye ma dang / a ga ru phye ma dang / spos kyi dmas pa thams cad kyi phyi ma'i sprin gyi mar ni rab tu bab/ lha'i bu mtha' yas pas kyang rang rang kyi lus kyi sprin ni shin tu
230a8(phal chen): dga' ldan gyi rigs su gtogs pa'i lha'i bu bye ba brgya stong brag bcu dang / re ma yin pa'i lha'i ris 'dus pa'i lha rnams kyis sems shin rung bas rjes rab su bskyed nas

230b4(phal chen): ga bkrol ba dang / brdungs pa'i tshogs grangs med pa yang sgra byin par gyur ro// lha'i bu dga' ldan gyi gnas na 'khod pa rnams dang / lha'i bu rnams kyis kyang bcom ldan la
230b5(phal chen): la ni lha/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung bar shin tu dkon par ni rjes su sems shing yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ni dam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa/ sgrib pa med pani
230b6(phal chen): chos can no zhes yang dag par song zhing de logs su mngon par yi rang ngo // dga' ldan gyi gnas nas khong pa'i 'khor thams cad dang / lha bye ba brgya stong grangs med pa bcom ldan
230b7(phal chen): 'das bsu ba'i phyir rin po che thams cad kyi me tog gi phur ma thogs pa dang / spos thams cad kyi phur sgrogs pa dang / rin po po che thams cad kyi phur ma thogs pa dang / rgyan thams
230b8(phal chen): cad kyi phur ma thogs pa dang / lha rdzas kyi tsan dang thams cad kyi phye ma'i phur ma thogs thogs pa dang / lha rdzas kyi a ga ru thams cad kyi phye ma'i phung ma thogs thogs pa dang /
231a1(phal chen): pa dang / lha rdzas kyi ring po che thams cad kyi bye ma'i bur ma thogs thogs pa dang / lha rdzas kyi spos kyi me tog thams cad kyi phye ma'i phung grogs
231a2(phal chen): pa dang / lha rdzas kyi me tog man+dAr ba'i phur ma thogs pa'i rnams kyang dong ste/ bcom ldan 'das gtor to// rab tu gtor to// lha'i bu dga' ldan gyi gnas su
231a3(phal chen): gtogs pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa rnams kyang bar snang la 'khod do ye shes kyi spyod yul la gzhol ba'i sems kyis gdugs pas bar snang
231a4(phal chen): brgyan pa byas so// sangs rgyas la dga' zhing gzhol ba'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi me tog thams cad kyi sbyin gyi char tu brgyan pas bar snang brgyan par byas/

231a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas la mchod par gsol ba'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi 'phreng ba sna tshogs kyi sbyin rab tu bkye bar snang brgyan par byas so// sangs rgyas kyi las tha

231a8(phal chen): so// de bzhin gshegs pa la yon tan gyi gnas dam pa yin par 'dzir pa'i sems kyis bre bre grangs me palas rin po tshethams cad kyis ma do'i rdzim
231b1(phal chen): zhing 'phrul pa'i brgyan gyis bar snang brgyan pa byas so// sangs rgyas la dge bar 'dun pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi gzhal med khang grangs med par sku rdzas kyi
231b2(phal chen): mo brdungs pa dang / bkrol ba thams cad kyi sgra yid du 'ong ba byung bas/ bar snang brgyan par byas so// sangs rgyas skye ba shin tu dkon par rigs pa'i sems kyis
231b3(phal chen): rnas kyin bza' kha dag sna tshogs kyi sbyin dang na brda' tshungs pa med pa'i sprin gyi char 'bab pa'i rkyen gyis bar sdang brgyan pa byas so// sangs rgyas la mos pa mtha' yas
231b4(phal chen): pa'i sems kyi grwa rdzas kyi cod pan grangs med pa'i sbyin las cod par gyi char chen po 'khor zhing 'bab pa'i rgyan gyis bar bar snang brgyan pa byas so// sangs rgyas la
231b5(phal chen): yid bde bar bskyed pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi rin po che kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa'i sprin las phreng ba sna tshogs kyi char rgyun mi 'chang bar 'bab pa'i rgyan gyis
231b6(phal chen): bar snang brgyan par byas so// lha'i bu bye ba brgya stong grangs med pa yang lha rdzas kyi me tog kha dog tha dad pa grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ me tog zad mi shes pa'i
231b7(phal chen): mdzod rab tu bkye nas/ bcom ldan 'das la mngon par gtor to/ mos pa'i spos zhim po rnyed cing sangs rgyas la dad par gnas pas lha rdzas kyi spos dang /

232a1(phal chen): med pa la gan thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das dag la mngon par gtor to// dga' ba'i sems kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi nabs 'bring du 'brang zhing

232a4(phal chen): kyis/ lha rdzas kyi rgyal mtshan rin po ches tshogs kyi kha dog can lag na thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs 'bring du 'ongs so// sangs rgyas dpa' ba mtha' yas
232a5(phal chen): pa rnam par 'phel ba'i sems kyi sku rdzas kyi sta ba lhub dang / 'phrul gyi la dog sa tshogs grangs med pa'i yang grangs med pa lag nathogs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la
232a6(phal chen): phul lo// dad pa mi phyogs pa'i sems kyi 'phreng ba grangs pA lag na thogs te bcom ldan 'das la mngon par gsel to// mtshungs pa med pa'i dga' ba rnam par 'phel bas
232a7(phal chen): sgra rdzas kyi bangan rin po che la dog sna tshogs grangs me pa la gan thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi drung nas 'dren to lha'i bu bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa yang rab tu
232a8(phal chen): gzhol zhing bag yod pa tshad med pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi rol mo brdung ba dang / dkrol ba la dag sna tshogs grangs med pa lags te/ yid du 'ong ba'i sgrang dbyangs phyung nas
232b1(phal chen): ldan 'das dgyes par byed de/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brdud du med pa dga' ldan nus nas 'ongs pa'i rnams kyang lha rdzas las 'das pa'i mchod pa 'ams
232b2(phal chen): gsum las par rnam par 'das pa dmigs pa'i chos las byung brjen pa'i dri ma med pa/ chags pa med pa'i sems tshim par byed pa/ chos zab mos mngon par grub pa/

232b8(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings brgyan par byas so// chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bur rtogs pa'i sems kyi lha rdzas las 'das pa'i spos thams cad kyi mchog gis gdug pa'i rgyan gyi

243a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas yod tan kun gyi 'byung gnas 'od mnga' ba// nor bur brtan par rab gshegs pa// ngas ni 'dir yang bkrags legs gyur cig/ ji ltar sna'i rgyal po
243a7(phal chen): ldan gyis sangs rgyas kyi mthus sngon gyi yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi yon tan brjod de// thub dkyang su tshigs su bca pas rgyas pa gshegs pa mdzes
243a8(phal chen): bsed pa 'is// 'jis chen gyi khams thams cadan yang // sa'i rgyal po bas 'asdamams sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis// klu'i dbya sus
243b1(phal chen): sngon gyi yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi yon tan brjod pa byed cing rgyal pa gshegs pa la'ang mngon par bskod do// de nas bcom ldan 'das chos kyi su ma su
243b2(phal chen): ma rnam par dag pa'i sku dang / 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas tha~Mb dang rigs gcig tu gyur pas par phul pa dang / chung
243b3(phal chen): gcig tu gyur pas sangs rgyas thas cad kyi rjes thug su chung pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang / nas tha cad la bsgribs pa med par khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi spyan dang / chos kyi mtha
243b4(phal chen): dbus med pa tri cad du sangs rgyas kyi byin brlabs rgyun mi chad pa dang / sems can 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du yongasu khyab pa'i sang rgyas kyi cho 'phrul dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku
243b5(phal chen): pa med pa'i rgyan gyis yang dag par brgyan pa dang / rgyas bzhin du byung ba'i chos bstan pa dang / byang chub sem dpa' brjod med pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing sna tshogs ras lhag pa'i la
243b6(phal chen): gyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i skus yang dag par spyod pa gnyisu med pa'i chos kyi sku la gnas pa'i sangs rgyas khyu mchog gi mthu phyung bas/ rin po che tham
243b7(phal chen): cad kyis brgyan pa'i khang par gsheg nas/ bdan bting ba la skyil mo dkrung bcas te bzhug so// ji ltar bco ldan 'das bzhugs pa bzhin du 'jig rten gyi lam tham cang du'ang ba
243b8(phal chen): par gyur te/ ji ltar bcom ldan 'dra rin po che tham cad kyi rgyan pa'i khang par gsheg pa dang / byon pa'i tshe sangs rgya kyi rim 'gro dang mchod pa byas shing rgyan gyi brgyan pa de dag blo cang pa de bani
244a1(phal chen): #/ gshegs pa de dag bzug pa'i tshe/ grangs par gyur pa dang / grangs med pa'i rnaM bar lha rdzas la 'dra ba'i me tog dang / 'phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / spos dang
244a2(phal chen): phye ma dang / na bza' dang / gtugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / rin po che dang / rol mo bcang ba dang / dkrol ba dang / glu dang / bstod pa dang / rjes dang / rim 'gro dang /
244a3(phal chen): dad pa dang / dga' ba dang / thal mo sbyar ba dang / lha rdzas zhes 'das pi rnam pa grangs med pa'i brgyan dang / lnga rdzas las 'das pa'i rnam pa grangs med pa'i bstod pa dang / lha rdzas
244a4(phal chen): 'das pa rnam pa grang med pa'i sprin gyi char 'bab pa/ lha rdzas las 'dra ba'i rnam pa grangs med pa'i gdugs gcig nas gcig tu brgyud te bsgreng ba dang / lha rdzas lnga 'ong ba'i grangs
244a5(phal chen): med pa'i rgyal mtshan la bdan sbyangs pa dang / shin tu srung ba grang med pas sbyar ba lnga rdzas lnga 'das pa'i yo byad kyi tshul dang / bsam pargya chen po rnam par 'phel bas/ sangs rgya
244a6(phal chen): mnyes par bya ba dang / mdzes pa'i rgyan rnam par dag pa dang / thams cad kyi rin po che'i dri thams cad dang / phyogs brgyan pa'i spos kyi sprin chen po dang / rol mo'i rnam pa sna tshogs rgyu
244a7(phal chen): tshe zhing yid du 'ong bas sangs rgyas la mchod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rim grol brtson pas// de bzhin gsheg pa'i gdan la bzug pa'i tshe/ grang med pA bar du mchod pa byas//
